Resolving the Italian-Ethiopian Dispute: Three Nations Continue Negotiations; Talks Are Only Exploratory and Have Not Reached the Level of Actual Politics; French Foreign Ministry Denies Italian Prime Minister's New Proposal; Italy Withdraws Troops from Libya, Easing the European Situation

(Rome) According to a semi-official spokesperson, the current negotiations among Paris, Rome, and London regarding the resolution of the Italian-Ethiopian dispute are merely of a general informative nature and lack a concrete plan as the basis for negotiation. Furthermore, according to inquiries by a Havas reporter, while the Italian government supports direct negotiations with Britain and France, it does not oppose resolving the Italian-Ethiopian issue within the League of Nations framework. Political figures believe that various compromises can be sought between direct negotiations and handling by the League of Nations. For example, the Chaco dispute between Paraguay and Bolivia was resolved through mediation by neighboring South American countries and then approved by the League of Nations Council. This shows that direct negotiations and League of Nations handling are not mutually exclusive. (Havas, 24th)

(London) Political circles here express the view that the general public earnestly hopes that the ongoing peace explorations between Paris and Rome will yield results within a few days, or that there will be legitimate reasons to postpone the implementation of sanctions when the Sanctions Coordination Committee meets on October 31 to decide the date for implementing sanctions. There is currently little evidence to confirm this hope. The diplomatic exchange of views is underway, with the British government being informed at all times, but it can be said that Britain is now merely an observer. It is currently believed here that French Prime Minister Laval also believes that the peace talks between Rome and Paris have not yet reached the stage of actual politics. (Reuters, 25th)

(London) Official sources state that the British government is prepared to implement financial and economic sanctions against Italy in early November, as a solution to the Italian-Ethiopian dispute may not be reached before the implementation of sanctions. Although Italy's proposal, transmitted through Paris, proves that Italy has made efforts in mediation, it cannot serve as a solid basis for future negotiations. Official sources believe that all proposals that advocate dividing Ethiopian territory into the core territory and conquered land (i.e., areas not belonging to the provinces of Amhara) and allowing these lands to remain under the rule of the Ethiopian Emperor are opposed by Britain in principle. This is because when Ethiopia requested to join the League of Nations in 1923, Italy had already recognized the territories conquered by former Ethiopian Emperor Menelik II, namely the provinces of Harar, Tigray, and Wollega, as Ethiopian territory. Apart from this, the most satisfactory action taken by Italy recently is the withdrawal of troops from Libya and their return to Italy, instead of stationing them in the colony of Tripolitania as originally planned. (Havas, 25th)

(Rome) Official sources state that the purpose of the negotiations among Britain, France, and Italy regarding the resolution of the Italian-Ethiopian dispute is to clarify the international atmosphere, determine the procedures for progress, and decide on the stance to be taken on fundamental issues. There is no definite plan yet. According to our reporter, this matter was initiated by a country not directly related to the Italian-Ethiopian dispute, which proposed suggestions to both parties so that each side could understand the other's views. These suggestions do not have a concrete form, and a concrete plan can only be proposed after the procedural issues are resolved. The procedural issues are of deep concern to Britain. Political figures here believe that with the upcoming British parliamentary elections, negotiations between Britain and Italy are difficult to conduct. Once the elections are over on November 14, an agreement to resolve the Italian-Ethiopian dispute can be announced in a short period of time. However, if the economic sanctions decided by the League of Nations are implemented, it may cause difficulties, which would require separate consideration. (Havas, 25th)

(Paris) Newspapers published news stating that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini had submitted a new proposal to Prime Minister Laval to resolve the Italian-Ethiopian dispute and that Laval had notified the British Ambassador to France, Clerk, this morning. The Foreign Ministry has since denied this, stating that it did not happen. (Havas, 24th)

(London) According to official announcements, French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval has already addressed the issue proposed by the Italian government. (Havas, 24th)

Contents of Alleged New Italian Proposal

(Paris) Although the British and French governments have denied the new proposal by the Italian government to resolve the Italian-Ethiopian dispute, the *L'Ere Nouvelle* newspaper here published the main points of this new proposal as follows: (1) Italy has decided to withdraw two divisions of troops stationed in Italian Libya and does not demand the withdrawal of British warships from the Mediterranean as an exchange condition. (2) Italy agrees to immediately cease hostilities once the British government submits a response. (3) Italy will not continue to send troops to East Africa before receiving the British response. (4) Italy suggests that if Britain deems it acceptable, it should be submitted to the League of Nations' Committee of Eighteen and the Council of Five. The Italian government believes that the above four suggestions are the country's greatest concessions. As for the content of Italy's demands, according to *L'Ere Nouvelle*, it does not advocate making the Ethiopian provinces of Harar, Wollega, and Tigray Italian protectorates or mandates, but only requests that these provinces be leased to Italy, preserving the nominal sovereignty of the Ethiopian Emperor. In addition, the international assistance plan previously proposed by the Committee of Five should be implemented within the core territory of Ethiopia. Italy also promises not to train indigenous troops in the leased territories mentioned above, but may organize police, whose number and equipment can be monitored by the signatories of the 1906 Tripartite Agreement, namely Britain, France, and Italy. In addition, Ethiopia may organize a standing army in its core territory, led by the Ethiopian Emperor, but all residents of the country should be disarmed. (Havas, 25th)

Withdrawal of Libyan Troops - A False Move

(Rome) It was officially announced here today that the government has ordered the withdrawal of a division of troops stationed in Libya. According to the official statement, this order is an independent action by the Italian government, and the British government has not made a similar commitment. (Reuters, 24th)

(Rome) It was officially announced here today that an Italian army division will be immediately withdrawn from Libya and returned to Italy, but Britain does not need to reduce the number of its naval vessels stationed in the Mediterranean in response. The diplomatic circles were very surprised by the peaceful tone of this announcement, as the general public believed that Italy would insist on an exchange condition. According to a Foreign Ministry spokesperson, this move should be seen as Italy's contribution to maintaining peace in Europe. (Guomin, 24th)

Naples: The Italian "Medo Division" currently stationed in Cyrenaica, Libya, Africa, has been ordered to return to Italy. The steamer "Sannia" has recently sailed to Libya to load the division's equipment. (Havas, 24th)

British Naval Redeployment in the Mediterranean

(London) The Admiralty officially announced today that the battleship HMS *Courageous* has departed from Alexandria, Egypt, today for Portsmouth. The battleship HMS *Ramillies* is scheduled to depart for Alexandria on November 1 to relieve the *Courageous*. (Guomin, 25th)

Malta, Valletta: Authorities here stated today that Britain does not intend to withdraw its fleet in the Mediterranean. The dispatch of the warships HMS *Hood* and HMS *Renown* to the Mediterranean when Italian troops were concentrating was purely a routine matter. Therefore, even if Italy withdraws a division of troops from Libya, it is unlikely to change Britain's naval policy. It is also learned today that the recent activity of Italian submarines in British territorial waters to make Britain decide not to withdraw any warships for the time being seems even more compelling. (Guomin, 25th)

League of Nations Coordination Committee Scheduled to Meet Next Thursday to Decide on Date for Implementing Sanctions; Hoare to Attend with Eden

(Geneva) The Secretary-General of the League of Nations recently notified the governments of the Covenant countries on behalf of the Coordination Committee that the Chairman of the Coordination Committee and the Committee of Eighteen, Visconde de Vasconcelos, has scheduled a meeting of the Committee of Eighteen at the League of Nations Secretariat at 10:30 AM on October 31, and a meeting of the Coordination Committee at 5:00 PM that afternoon. (Central News Agency, 24th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly's Committee of Eighteen on Sanctions is scheduled to continue its meeting here on October 31. It is reported that British Foreign Secretary Hoare and Minister Without Portfolio Eden will come to attend, but French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval may not have time to attend due to busy domestic affairs. (Havas, 24th)

China's Notification to the League of Nations; Reply Has Not Yet Been Issued

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic sources, China is still considering its response to the League of Nations' notification regarding economic sanctions against Italy, so a reply has not yet been issued. As for rumors that a reply will be given to the League of Nations before the 28th, it is said that there is no definitive provision in the League of Nations' notification. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

League of Nations Sanctions Issue; White House Discussing Reply; Will Reiterate Actions Taken Under Neutrality Law; Decided to Stay Out of the Italian-Ethiopian Dispute

(Washington) It is reported that President Roosevelt and Secretary of State Hull agreed today on the wording of the reply to the League of Nations regarding the sanctions against Italy. According to reliable sources, the reply will only reiterate the actions taken by the United States under the Neutrality Law and will not comment on the League of Nations' proposal to end the Italian-Ethiopian War. (Reuters, 24th)

(Washington) According to reliable sources, Secretary of State Hull met with President Roosevelt today to discuss the United States' attitude towards the League of Nations' implementation of sanctions against Italy and the issue of the US representatives at the London Naval Conference. Hull had lunch with the President at the White House today, and the main topic of discussion was the reply to the League of Nations on the sanctions issue. The President and Hull paid close attention to the issue of banning arms exports to Italy, and government advisors also disagreed. According to the Neutrality Law passed by Congress, it is difficult to determine whether the President has the power to announce this ban. (Guomin, 24th)

(Washington) Since the State Department received the League of Nations' memorandum on sanctions against Italy, President Roosevelt has discussed with Secretary of State Hull three times how to respond. Because the authorities are keeping the matter secret, the outside world knows nothing. Hull has also had long talks with State Department officials, but has not consulted experts on wartime neutrality laws. Some people have therefore concluded that the State Department has not yet drafted a reply and will not submit a reply to the League of Nations before the beginning of next week. (Havas, 24th)

Sharp Increase in US Exports to Italy

(Washington) The Department of Commerce announced today that US exports of chemicals and related products in September totaled $12,030,000, compared to $10,884,000 in September 1934. Exports of naval stores totaled $1,618,200, an increase of $291,550 compared to the same period a year ago. Most of these naval stores were shipped to Italy, resulting in a 15% increase in US exports to Italy. US rubber exports for the first nine months of this year totaled $16,369,676, less than the exports for the same period last year, which totaled $16,547,214. (Guomin, 24th)

Implementing League of Nations Resolution; Britain Bans Arms Shipments to Italy; Regulations Issued, Licenses Revoked

(London) Foreign Secretary Hoare issued regulations today strictly prohibiting the shipment of arms and ammunition to Italy. (Guomin, 25th)

(London) The Board of Trade issued a bulletin stating that all licenses for transporting arms to Italy have been revoked in accordance with the resolution of the Geneva Sanctions Committee. (Havas, 25th)

Third Day of British House of Commons Session; Foreign Policy Debate Concludes; Fifty Nations Reaffirm Public Law; Aggressors Will Ultimately Be Difficult to Sustain; Attention Called to German Rearmament, Considered More Serious Than Italian-Ethiopian Conflict; Churchill's Eloquent Speech

(London) Today was the third and final day of the House of Commons debate on international events. The highlight of the session was Churchill's brilliant speech, which was applauded by the entire House. Home Secretary Simon spoke on behalf of the government, concluding the debate, mostly focusing on domestic achievements. After the debate, no vote was taken. Churchill began by drawing attention to the extent and speed of German rearmament, stating that Germany had spent £800 million on direct and indirect military preparations, a figure almost unbelievable. Regardless of the reasons or purposes of these actions, he felt that there was nothing more concerning. Compared to the Italian-Ethiopian War, the Italian-Ethiopian conflict was a minor matter. We must consider the Italian-Ethiopian dispute in light of German rearmament. He believed that in all circumstances, France's efforts to implement the League of Nations Covenant deserved our fervent recognition. Churchill also said that Germany's re-entry into the League of Nations was the most precious goal that Britain had strived to achieve. He was confident that Britain would never engage in another war that contradicted the League of Nations Covenant. Therefore, if the British Empire had to defend itself, then British imperialism and League of Nations principles would be one and the same, not two separate things. He expressed sympathy for Ethiopia's invasion, but since Ethiopia had appealed to the League of Nations, the League should manage its affairs, so that the League would not be accused of favoring one side against Italy. The League of Nations is still alive and active, which is a new and significant development in the international situation. The League of Nations is currently fighting for its survival and almost for the survival of us all. Fifty nations have reaffirmed public law, which is a memorable event for us. What is particularly noteworthy is Mussolini's compliance with sanctions and maintaining contact with the League of Nations, which is a sign of the Italian Prime Minister's breadth of mind and one of the Italian Prime Minister's strongest achievements. The League of Nations has now moved from shadow to substance, from empty talk to practice. Its structure was magnificent and splendid before, but in reality, it had only form without substance. Today, it has power covering its body. We are gradually realizing that the League of Nations will one day bless the world with an even stronger and safer plan. He asked the House of Commons not to think that the current sanctions plan was not severe enough. We cannot take a short-sighted view of the next one or two months. Who knows, in a year, hundreds of thousands of Italian troops might be deeply entrenched in Ethiopia, and rapidly die from disease and guerrilla warfare. Italy is now bleeding from every pore under the world's boycott and condemnation. Gold reserves are dwindling, prices are rising, and credit is failing. How can it last for long? No matter how difficult and dangerous, only those who persevere will ultimately win. We must quickly secure a safe and lasting control of the Mediterranean. Former Health Minister Greenwood then spoke, accusing the government of using international issues to divert the public's attention, so that the public would no longer pay attention to the government's failed unemployment relief policies. Simon rose to conclude the debate, only mentioning one thing regarding international events, saying that a strange message had been sent out this morning, claiming that London, Paris, and Rome now had a scheme to submit a fait accompli to the League of Nations, which would harm the interests of one party and violate the principles of the League of Nations. It is important to know that this accusation is completely false. We are not now running counter to the League of Nations, and have never had the idea of doing so. We also do not want to abandon our collective obligations under the League of Nations Covenant. We certainly hope for a quick and complete solution, but this solution must not fall outside the scope of the League of Nations structure and must be acceptable to both Italy and Ethiopia and the League of Nations itself. Simon continued to speak about domestic affairs and said that British exports to Italy had decreased, not due to sanctions, but due to the Italians' lack of financial resources. (Reuters, 24th)

Parliament Dissolved, Awaiting Re-election; The King Personally Delivers Address; Deeply Regrets That Peace Efforts Failed to Avert War; Expresses Satisfaction That Domestic Economy Is Gradually Moving Towards Prosperity

(London) This morning at 11:00, the House of Lords and the House of Commons held their last meeting. No official business was conducted. Members of the House of Commons were then summoned to the House of Lords to respectfully listen to the King's address regarding the dissolution of Parliament, which read in part: This year marks the 25th anniversary of my reign, and I and the Queen will always remember this as one of the happiest anniversaries. The expressions of loyalty and love from all sides are unforgettable. The Prime Ministers of the Dominions and the representatives of India were welcomed by me to participate in the celebrations. My relations with foreign countries continue to be friendly. Unfortunately, events occurred between Italy and Ethiopia, to which I have paid the greatest attention. Since the border conflict occurred in East Africa last December, my government has done its utmost, either individually or together with the member states of the League of Nations, to promote a peaceful resolution. It is a matter of regret to me that all these efforts ultimately failed to prevent the use of force. However, my government still faithfully supports the League of Nations' plan to restore peace and establish a friendly resolution in the spirit of the Covenant. I have approved the Act regarding the future political systems of India and Burma. This Act will surely be one of the most important and complex projects that Parliament has ever handled in the records of both houses. When this Act is implemented in the future, it will not only bring comfort and happiness to the people of India and Burma but will also make the friendly relations between India and Burma and other parts of my Empire even closer. As for domestic affairs, the gradual recovery of industry, the increase in national income, and the effectiveness of financial management have created a great progress towards prosperity. My government is now able to exempt the additional taxes imposed four years ago, and can provide full relief to small taxpayers, which is a source of satisfaction to me. It is also pleasing to me that the number of unemployed has gradually decreased over the past year. Although there are various unfavorable conditions in the position of international trade, our country's overseas trade is still expanding, and business is particularly prosperous with other parts of my Empire and countries that have concluded commercial treaties. My government is constantly striving to conclude international agreements to limit various armaments, but it now feels the need to expand the air force to strengthen our defenses, and the implementation process is now underway. After the address was read, Parliament was adjourned. (Reuters, 25th)

Italy Uses Radio to Conduct Anti-British Propaganda in the Near East; London Lodges Representations

(London) Recently, the Italian radio station has been broadcasting anti-British propaganda to the Arab and Muslim peoples in the Near East. When the House of Commons met today, a member asked the government about this matter. Overseas Dominions Secretary Thomas replied that the government had made representations to the Italian government on this matter and that Britain would soon establish a radio broadcasting station in Palestine. (Havas, 24th)

Amidst the Italian-Ethiopian War, There is Talk of a Franco-German Rapprochement

(Paris) The complex situation of the Italian-Ethiopian peace agreement and the internal political situation in France has been further complicated today by talk of a Franco-German rapprochement. Paris *Echo* columnist Bertin and *Volffre* reporter Tapia both stated today that France recently had an informal representative visit German leader Hitler. Bertin also said that Hitler was quite indifferent to Franco-German friendship, because of all the countries, Hitler would rather have friendly relations with Britain. Tapia stated that Hitler's personal representative, Liedrohof, may come to France in the future. (Guomin, 24th)

US Merchants Reduce Marine War Insurance Rates; Sign of Easing European Situation

(New York) Marine insurance merchants here now believe that the European situation is clearly easing and have reduced war insurance rates today. (Guomin, 24th)

No War on Eastern Front; Ethiopian Troops Once Attacked the Aduwa Right Flank; Italian Aircraft Reconnoitered 3,000 Miles of the Northern Route

(Rome) The Propaganda Department issued its 27th bulletin, stating that there was no war on the Tigray province and Wogga-Dan front in Ethiopia. Ethiopian natives have been flocking to the Italian army, so Italian outposts have been able to advance along the Adigrat-Adua and Aksum lines. (Havas, 24th)

Addis Ababa An unconfirmed report received here today states that Italian forces are advancing northwest towards Walwal, aiming for the town of Sassabane, 140 miles from Harar. It is said that the Italian objective is to cut off several central garrison points by encircling the Ethiopian army's lines. This includes Gora Hai, an Ethiopian communication hub. They also aim to break through the enemy lines from the rear. Another report states that tens of thousands of soldiers are gathering in valleys and passes, waiting to resist the Italian army led by Graziani. (Reuters, 24th)

Addis Ababa Thousands of Ethiopian troops marched north today, preparing for a decisive battle, which is expected to occur soon. (National Telegram, 25th)

(Rome) According to dispatches from Asmara, Eritrea, Ethiopian forces under General Seyoum attacked the Italian right flank on the Aduwa line today but were repulsed. General Seyoum is now withdrawing his troops to the Chila River, a tributary of the Tekeze River. Italian vanguards on the southern front are halting the Ethiopian advance in Mai Tzehel. According to Ethiopian prisoners, the Ethiopian forces on that front are awaiting reinforcements from Addis Ababa before launching a general offensive. It is reported that the reinforcements have two bomber aircraft. Today, a public statement claimed that Italian reserve forces have occupied the village of Galafó, a major neutral point in the Shilille area on the southern front. (Havas, 25th)

Asmara Major Barnes, a Reuters correspondent accompanying Count Ciano, Mussolini's son-in-law, and his squadron of aircraft, sent a cable today detailing the Italian aircraft's reconnaissance of enemy troops over 3,000 miles of the northern front. It was reported that an Ethiopian machine gun squad was spotted in a certain area. The aircraft flew to within a few hundred feet of the ground and strafed the Ethiopian troops with machine gun fire. The Ethiopian troops also returned fire with machine guns, but none of the Italian aircraft were damaged. The main purpose of the Italian aircraft's reconnaissance was to determine the location of General Seyoum's troops, but no large gatherings of Ethiopian soldiers were seen. Therefore, the location of the enemy's main force has not yet been discovered. (Reuters, 25th)

Harar According to a cable from our correspondent La Foya, Ethiopian regular troops, trained by Belgian instructors, have recently departed from Qiqiqa City (east of Harar) for the Wogga-Dan area. General Nasibu, the governor of Harar province and commander-in-chief of the southern front, has also departed for Qiqiqa City, where he will establish his headquarters to command the southern military operations. Before the departure of these troops, General Nasibu personally reviewed them. This was greatly welcomed by the local people. This is an elite Ethiopian force, including infantry, machine gun squads, and 300 cavalrymen in bright uniforms. In addition, there is a camel corps, which was trained by Belgian instructors in the last six months. Military, political, and religious dignitaries were all present at the review. General Nasibu, fully armed, sat high on a white horse, presenting a remarkable figure. He delivered an enthusiastic speech to the troops. After listening to the speech, the troops marched out of the city in a cloud of dust. Women lined the streets to bid farewell to the soldiers, showering them and their banners with flowers. (Havas, 25th)

Addis Ababa According to a cable from our correspondent O'Chona, General Gedashu and General Mariam recently led their troops from the Wollega province to the capital, where they are about to depart for the front lines. They were recently reviewed by the Ethiopian Emperor. The troops were making a cacophony of sounds with horns and pipes. A black band played Slavic music. Flags were crossed, indicating the positions of various chieftains. Crowds gathered before the chieftains, cheering and supporting them. However, the troops were not lined up neatly. Officers often struck them with wooden sticks to make them stand at attention and "dress ranks." The Emperor arrived at 11:30 AM to review 40,000 of these old-style soldiers, each carrying different weapons. Although they had been marching for ten days, they showed no signs of fatigue. General Gedashu, smiling, first paid his respects to the Emperor and then addressed the troops, urging his subordinates to be brave and cautious. (Havas, 25th)

Addis Ababa According to a cable from our correspondent O'Chona, a hand grenade factory organized by Armenian Savolin, employing 40 workers, is about to begin production. It is expected to produce 1,000 hand grenades per day. The grenades are oblong and weigh 300 grams each. They can be thrown 50 meters and have a blast radius of 10 meters. (Havas, 25th)

Unrest Among Black Natives on British West Indian Islands; Filled With Resentment Against Italian Aggression

(London) The Times recently published an article by Sir Bell, stating that "riots have broken out among the black people of St. Vincent, a British island in the West Indies, and are widespread. These riots are likely the result of Italy's aggression against Abyssinia. Since Italy launched its aggression against Abyssinia, everywhere in Africa, in the tents of Nigerian chiefs, in the gatherings of native merchants, in the marketplaces of villages and towns, and in the everyday conversations of Equatorial Africa, this unjust war is being discussed. Previously, the people of [British] colonies deeply believed in the honor and justice of [the British] nation based on all the facts. However, the Italo-Ethiopian affair has caused resentment and deep suspicion in their hearts. It should be understood that collective security is the best principle, but what the world needs most is collective justice." Sir Bell has served as the governor of British colonies in the West Indies, Africa, and the Indian Ocean. (Havas, 25th)

Pacific Airmail to Officially Begin Next Spring; Temporarily Ending at the Philippine Islands and the Far East; Completion of the Trial Flight of the "Clipper"

(New York) It was learned here today that Pacific Aviation will begin carrying passengers to Manila for the first time in mid-January of next year. At the same time, a trial flight from Alameda, California, to Manila will take place in early November, with stops at Honolulu, Midway Island, Wake Island, and Guam. (National Telegram, 24th)

(Washington) The Post Office Department announced today that the right to operate the Pacific airmail service from San Francisco to the Far East has been granted to Pan American Airways. Deputy Postmaster General W. Bulen Thaw said that Manila will temporarily be the Far East terminus of the air route, from which mail will be transferred to mail ships for delivery to Guangzhou. The postage rate between the United States and China will be approximately one U.S. dollar per half ounce. (National Telegram, 24th)

Alameda The fourth trial flight of the "Clipper" large aircraft across the Pacific has been completed today. It arrived safely here at 11:01 AM this morning after departing from Honolulu yesterday afternoon. (National Telegram, 24th)

Decline in Shanghai Silver Coin Value; U.S. Treasury Secretary Makes No Comment

Revolution Breaks Out on the Greek Island of Crete; Monarchist Movement Provokes Repercussions

Athens A revolution broke out on the island of Crete today. The government immediately dispatched troops to suppress it and prevent it from spreading elsewhere. Crete has not been peaceful since the revolution last July. The island is a stronghold of the Republican Party. Recently, the monarchist movement has been gaining momentum in various parts of Greece, which has provoked repercussions on the island. (National Telegram, 24th)

In the Midst of Calls to Reopen Naval Conference, Britain, the United States, and Japan Hold Divergent Views; US Advocates a 5:5:3 Ratio, Japan Advocates Equality; Britain Wants to Expand the Scope to Include Germany and Russia

(London) First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell declared in the House of Commons today that the government has sent notes to Washington and the signatory countries of the London Naval Treaty—the United States, France, Italy, and Japan—inquiring whether they would send representatives to the naval conference to be held in London on December 2nd. The purpose of the conference is to strive as much as possible to agree on all matters concerning naval limitations, so as to conclude an international treaty to replace the two naval treaties that will expire at the end of 1936. The government is also consulting with the Dominions on this matter. It is now hoped that representatives from the signatory countries can agree to expand the scope of the conference to allow other naval powers to join. (Reuters, 24th)

(Washington) The State Department officially announced today that the United States has accepted Britain's invitation to send representatives to the London Naval Conference on December 2nd and has sent a cable to U.S. Ambassador to Britain Bingham informing British Foreign Secretary Hoare of this. The original letter of invitation has not yet been received here, but after consulting with Secretary of State Hull and President Roosevelt, the decision was made to accept based on Bingham's cable. It is also understood that the United States will abandon its past policy this time, not sending diplomats as representatives, but appointing Rear Admiral Standley, the head of the Navy Department's Planning Division, who has always advocated a large navy, as the chief representative. Davis, who has represented the United States at international conferences in the past, will not be going to London this time. Standley met with President Roosevelt for about half an hour today. Afterwards, Standley stated that he and the President had discussed the general situation regarding naval issues. (National Telegram, 24th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the British government's convening of a disarmament conference, the Japanese government is preparing to consider the selection of representatives. However, recently, the U.S. Secretary of the Navy declared opposition to revising the 5:5:3 ratio, and the British Prime Minister strongly argued for the necessity of supplementing military equipment. France, Italy, and other countries also advocate military expansion. If the disarmament conference proceeds in the face of such pessimistic [views on] disarmament, there must be new proposals to prevent the danger of the conference collapsing. Although Japan will participate in the conference, it will never change its long-held disarmament policy. After receiving the British government's official invitation, it intends to convey this intention to the British government to avoid misunderstandings. (Domei News Agency, 24th)

(Tokyo) The British government's official invitation for a disarmament conference was delivered to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs by Chargé d'Affaires Fujii on the 25th. The contents of the invitation are being kept strictly secret. According to reliable sources, the British government did not reveal any specific items on the agenda, but merely stated that the British government has consistently adopted a gentlemanly attitude since the preliminary consultations. Therefore, based on the Washington and London treaties, it will convene a formal conference in London starting on December 2nd. The conference is intended to establish a fair and appropriate new international treaty to replace the two old treaties of Washington and London. It also needs to consult with all parties as much as possible on naval limitation issues in order to achieve its objectives. If there is hope of reaching an agreement with the countries concerned, other countries will also be invited. Regarding the composition of the delegation, it is only hoped that the organization will be small. However, the circumstances regarding the country's proposed declaration of autonomous shipbuilding and the use of qualitative restrictions as the basis of the conference were not mentioned. (United Press, 25th)

British Aircraft Arrives in Hong Kong From Singapore

(Hong Kong) The British Imperial Airways aircraft "Doradus," piloted by Captain Armytage, arrived here at 5:00 PM today. It took about ten hours from Singapore to Hong Kong, with brief stops at Penang and Tourane en route. It landed safely despite heavy rain at the time of arrival. (Reuters, 24th)

Hurricane Passes Through Qingdao

(Qingdao) A hurricane passed through here early this morning, causing serious damage. The "Haihua" (transliteration) ship ran aground near the entrance of the port due to the wind. Several civilian ships were overturned. It is now known that three people have died and thirty are missing. The hurricane came from the north and then blew towards the southeast. Many trees along the coast were uprooted, and roofs and telephone lines were blown down and scattered across the streets. (Reuters, 25th)

Renwan Embankment on the North Bank of the Beitang River in Guanyun Collapses

(Huaiyin) According to the flood control office, the Renwan embankment on the north bank of the Beitang River in Guanyun collapsed for more than ten zhang [a Chinese unit of length, approximately 3.3 meters] due to wind and rain overnight on the 24th. The county town is in critical condition. Merchants and residents guarded throughout the night. County Magistrate Xu led the security team leader Tao Baiyang, the police chief Huang Guizhou, and the first district chief Hu Cheng, etc., to supervise the soldiers and police officers to desperately protect the area around the Great King Temple outside the West Gate and the embankment itself. There is also news that the Youwan Zong Liutangkou, on the border of Si and Su counties, is in danger. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Xu Prefecture Requests Funds From the Province to Deal With Famine Relief

(Xuzhou) The Prefecture sent a telegram to the province, stating that the breach of the Peidong Dike has expanded the disaster area. In addition to supervising the blockade, it is rushing to arrange emergency relief. It is requested that the Provincial Relief Committee allocate funds for emergency assistance. If the remittance is delayed, it is proposed to first allocate 6,000 yuan from the remaining disaster relief and Huai River travel expenses to meet urgent needs. It has been found that the northeast wind caused the greatest damage to the western dike of Weishan Lake. Fortunately, the northern dike of Tongfeng was preserved, but the defending forces are exhausted. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Xuzhou) Shao Hanyuan sent a telegram to the province, stating that winter is approaching, and the disaster victims are eating in the open and sleeping in the dew, crying from hunger and cold, which is unbearable to witness. It is requested that the Relief Committee quickly determine a relief policy, continue to allocate relief funds, and send personnel to Xuzhou to distribute [supplies]. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Wind and Rain Stopped Yesterday Morning; Fortunately, Pei City Was Not Affected by the Disaster

(Xuzhou) There have been several days of heavy wind and rain in northern Xuzhou. The western dike of Weishan Lake and all the surrounding dikes are unstable. A section of the dike north of Donggao Small Lake in Pei City collapsed, and efforts to block it were ineffective. Around 11:00 PM on the 24th, a breach of more than 100 meters occurred, and the floodwaters rushed in violently. The flood head was only two or three li [a Chinese unit of distance, approximately 500 meters] from Pei City. The water flowing backwards was especially fierce. According to a telegram from the Magistrate of Pei County, the Prefecture has ordered the urgent protection of the county town and the speedy rescue of the disaster victims. Fortunately, the wind and rain stopped this morning, and the lake water receded. The disaster area may not expand further, and Pei City may be preserved. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Snow and Hail in Kangzhuang

Chaotic Situation in Xianghe; Mobs Still Hold Political Power; No Military or Police in the City Except for the Militia; Rumors Rampant in Wuqing, Sanhe, and Other Places; Shang Zhen Visits Tada, Sakai, and Others to Discuss Solutions

(Beiping) Shang Zhen went to Tianjin last night. This morning, he met with Tada Shun, Commander of the Japanese North China Garrison Army, and Chief of Staff Sakai Takashi, in Tianjin. In the afternoon, he visited Takeshita, the head of the Yuguan Special Affairs Agency, and others to discuss solutions to the Xianghe incident. It is said that the result was satisfactory. It was agreed that he would return to Beiping in a day or two. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Tianjin) The Hu Battalion of the 175th Regiment of the 32nd Army, which was dispatched to Xianghe City to maintain order, has retreated to the suburbs to avoid conflict with the rioters. The city is still controlled by the rioters, including Wu Zhenyi, who was self-appointed as the head of the Public Security Bureau, and other section chiefs, issuing orders. Jiang De'en, the deputy head of the militia, has joined the rioters. Reactionary and absurd slogans are posted everywhere in the city, and rioters frequently march with flags. It is reported that the real farmers have long since scattered, and those participating are all gangsters from Shi Yousan and Liu Guitang, disguised as civilians and hiding weapons, machine guns, etc. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) The plan for the Xianghe rebellion has been obtained by the Jixian County government. It will take some time to resolve this matter. Shops in Xianghe City have now been forced to open. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Tianjin) Shang Zhen came to Tianjin on the night of the 24th. According to reports, in addition to inspecting local security, he also plans to meet with Tada and Takeshita. The Xianghe incident must find a proper diplomatic solution. This incident occurred because a small number of treacherous people hijacked the people's will and had other intentions, using tax reduction as an excuse to cause chaos. Changping and Wuqing are on high alert and will not be affected. With the country in such a state and traitors everywhere, it is impossible to guard against them, which is truly lamentable. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) According to Tongxian, after the Xianghe people were incited by a certain party and caused a rebellion, the authorities here learned from reports from various counties that the farmers in Sanhe County in the Ji-Mi area, as well as the neighboring Baodi, Wuqing, and Changping counties, are also unstable, but the situation is not serious. The 7th Company of the 1st Security Regiment, which was dispatched to Xianghe to suppress [the rebellion] on the 23rd, returned to its original defense in Sanhe this morning because the Shang Army had arrived to take over. The Ji-Mi Regional Office has ordered the security teams stationed in various counties to be on high alert to prevent villains from taking advantage of the opportunity to disrupt public order. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) According to visitors from Xianghe, the 1st Company of the 1st Regiment, led by Zhang Qingyu, which was stationed in Xianghe City, has been transferred from Xianghe County to Sanhe County due to the tight defense situation in Sanhe, Baodi, and other counties in the war zone. There are now no military or police stationed in Xianghe City except for the local militia. The 32nd Army's Hu Bin Battalion had three companies that attempted to go to Xianghe, but they returned midway. Although Xianghe City has entered a state of anarchy, the order is not chaotic. The local people are panicking. The background of this incident is complex, and our authorities will resolve it appropriately. In addition, due to the impact of the Xianghe incident, rumors are rampant in Wuqing, Sanhe, Baodi, and other places. Local defenses are tight, and the authorities have ordered strict vigilance in various places. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Tianjin) Shang Zhen visited Cheng Ke at 5:00 PM on the 25th to discuss local security. Regarding the Xianghe incident, the Civil Affairs Department telegraphed Tianjin on the 25th, stating that Anci and Wuqing are as peaceful as ever. Changping's security is being maintained by Feng's troops, and the rioters have no opportunity to take advantage [of the situation]. Shang completed negotiations with the relevant parties in Tianjin and will go to Beiping within the next day or two. (Central News Agency, 25th)

(Beiping) The situation in the Xianghe incident is extremely complex. The provincial authorities have now decided to handle it with diplomatic and political tactics. Shang Zhen is currently in Tianjin negotiating. It may be possible to quell [the rebellion] within days. The Xianghe regime is still in the hands of the rioters. Deputy County Magistrate Liu Yaodong is also still detained. Liu's entourage was killed. Two companies of the 2nd Battalion of the 32nd Army withdrew from Xianghe on the 25th. It is reported that the bandits do have a conspiracy, and the scope is quite broad. They are also advocating for the "Four Powers Movement" and implementing democracy. Fortunately, they were discovered early and will not succeed. (Central News Agency, 25th)

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan received a telegram from Shang Zhen, Chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, on the morning of the 25th, reporting the details of the Xianghe incident, stating that it was instigated by traitors and a certain foreign ronin. Troops were dispatched to suppress [the rebellion]. The rebels have scattered, and it can be completely resolved within days. The Executive Yuan has sent a telegram to commend [Shang Zhen] and has provided detailed instructions. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Liu Yaodong is Detained

(Beiping) Liu Yaodong, a counselor of the Hebei Provincial Government, was dispatched to Xianghe to investigate and act as deputy county magistrate. Upon arrival in Xianghe, he was detained by the rebels. Liu has now been moved by the rebels from the city to a certain village in the eastern countryside of the county. His whereabouts are unknown. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Tianjin) Liu Yaodong, a counselor dispatched to Xianghe by the Provincial Government, was immediately placed under house arrest at Kuishun Inn, losing his freedom. Traffic in the city remains cut off. The rioters hold several meetings a day, with many disputes and arguments. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Zhang Qingyu Returns to Tong After Meeting With Shang

(Beiping) Zhang Qingyu, commander of the War Zone Security 1st Regiment, came to Beiping yesterday to meet with Shang Zhen and report on everything. Due to the heavy war zone defense duties, he returned to Tong this morning to take command. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) Zhang Qingyu, commander of the 1st Security Regiment, and Li Yunsheng, commander of the 5th Security Regiment, returned to Tong on the morning of the 24th to command everything. Feng Shoupeng, commander of the 3rd Battalion of the Hebei Security 5th Regiment, stationed in Changping, came to Beiping yesterday and met with Shang Zhen today to report on the recent situation of the defense. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) Zhang Jianyun and another person dispatched by the Ji-Mi Regional Office to Xianghe to investigate the truth of the incident came to Beiping from Tong this morning to report on the investigation to the relevant authorities. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

The Secret Plotting of the Rebel Riot

(Beiping) According to people from Xianghe, the rebellion in Xianghe was initiated by rebel leaders An Houqi and Wu Yiting. An and others had previously been living in Beiping. On the 15th, they went from Beiping to Xianghe. At An Houzhai's home in Lingzi Village, outside the east gate of the county, they gathered more than 20 ronin to secretly plot the riot. Starting on the 16th, they held meetings day and night at Hu Chengwu's home in Anfu Fuzhai. On the 20th, they gathered more than 1,000 ignorant villagers outside the city, intending to enter the city. On the 21st, the rebels sent six representatives, including three ronin and three Chinese—Chen Zhiru, Cao Fuqing, and Zhang Yizhai—into the city to demand the county magistrate Zhao's seal. They were driven out. The ronin were temporarily detained at the Chengxing Shop on South Main Street of the county government, and the Chinese Chen Zhiru, etc., were detained at the Kuishun Inn. The Japanese Embassy's military police heard the news and sent more than 20 military police, led by Captain Otaki, to arrive at Yihe on the night of the 22nd. The four gates of the county were closed and sandbags were piled up to prevent the rioters from attacking the city. When the military police entered the city through the west gate that day, they took the three ronin. At the same time, the three Chinese also disappeared. The rebels, seeing that the Japanese military police had entered the city, opened the city gate and poured into the city, completely robbing the Public Security Bureau's police and firearms. Bai Zhichun, the head of the Public Security Bureau, and squad leader Liu Chen, etc., jumped off the wall of Kuixing [Inn] in Dongguan in an attempt to escape. They were injured upon landing and then severely beaten by the rebels, suffering serious injuries. After the incident in Xianghe, militia chief Jiang Enliang and Chamber of Commerce president Wang Futing came forward to maintain local security. County Magistrate Zhao Chongpu fled with the seal on the 22nd. The rebels chased after him, but turned back at Ganshuiba, ten li from the county, when they failed to catch him. (Special Dispatch, 24th)

Takahashi Arrives in Beiping and Makes a Statement

(Beiping) Takahashi, the military attaché of the Japanese Embassy, returned to Beiping from Tianjin last night. This morning, he made a statement saying that he left Beiping on the 19th to go to Shanghai to attend a meeting of military attachés stationed in China, convened by Major General Okamura in Shanghai. The meeting was held for two days on the 20th and 21st, during which Okamura conveyed the Army Department's intentions towards China, and military attachés from various places in North China, Southwest China, and Central China reported on the local situation and exchanged thorough opinions. He left Shanghai on the 23rd on a China National Aviation Corporation plane and returned to Tianjin to visit Commander Tada and report on the Shanghai meeting. The Shanghai meeting did not discuss any proposals. Recent rumors have been rampant, but they are the idle talk of alarmists and are not true. He had only learned about the Xianghe incident after reporting [back] to Beiping. According to investigations, no Japanese were involved. However, Xianghe is a non-combat zone demilitarized area, and Chinese troops are not allowed to enter the city. If the unrest can be quelled, it will be the responsibility of the Chinese government. He was not familiar with other details. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) Takahashi said: (1) The Shanghai Japanese military attaché meeting was held for only two days, the 20th and 21st. After military attachés reported on the situations in North China, South China, and Sichuan and Shaanxi, Okamura conveyed the intentions of the Japanese military department, and they exchanged opinions, reaching complete agreement. There were no other important discussions. (2) He was not yet familiar with the details of the Xianghe incident. According to his observation, it was a kind of popular movement. The Japanese side sent people to investigate because the area was a war zone demilitarized area, but had no other intentions. (Central News Agency, 25th)

Dai Kui-sheng Reports on Work to the President of the Academy

(Nanjing) Central Committee Member and Supervisory Commissioner of the Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai Region, Dai Kui-sheng, came to Nanjing to meet with President of the Control Yuan, Yu Youren, to report on his work. Dai said that the implementation of the supervisory system in the three provinces of Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai has received the sympathy and facilitation of the local authorities in each province. He himself will submit two proposals to the congress together with Chairman Shao and Chairman Zhu Shuming. Shao and Zhu will come to Nanjing at the end of the month to attend. Deputy Commander Zhang in Shaanxi will also come to Nanjing in early November. He will return to Gansu immediately after the closing of the congress. (Special dispatch from the 25th)

Jiang Zuobin Reschedules Return to China

(Nanjing) Ambassador to Japan Jiang, originally scheduled to return to China on the 24th, has now rescheduled to take the Empress of Asia liner on the 31st due to unfinished official business in Japan. The journey is estimated to take until November 4th to reach Shanghai. (Special dispatch from the 25th)

Ju Zheng Thanks Chairman Chiang Kai-shek by Telegram

(Nanjing) President of the Judicial Yuan, Ju Zheng, celebrated his sixtieth birthday on the 20th. Chairman Chiang sent a telegram to congratulate him, saying, "Unable to personally attend to offer congratulations on Mr.'s sixtieth anniversary, [you are] a pillar of the party and the nation, wishing you health and good fortune, boundless happiness," etc. Ju Zheng stated on the 24th that "Being in my old age, I am all the more mindful of the precepts of virtue, and I am grateful for your kindness and praise. Reflecting on the fleeting time, my feeling of inadequacy only increases. I hereby send a telegram to express my thanks and wish the party well." (Special dispatch from the 25th)

(2) Negotiating with the Ministry of Railways to inspect state-run railway factories. (3) Dispatching personnel to assist Jiangsu Province in carrying out factory inspections in Wuxi. (4) Urging Anhui Province to conduct factory and mine inspections. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 25th)

Criminal Impersonating a Military Officer Apprehended in Nanjing

Jiangsu Provincial Government Held Routine Meeting Yesterday

(Zhenjiang) The Jiangsu Provincial Government resolved at its routine meeting on the 25th: (1) To pass the general outline of measures for the rice stem borer control campaign in various counties for the 24th year. (2) The previously established case of exempting newly cultivated land from taxation for three years will be cancelled from this year onwards because the collection is prone to corruption. In order to prevent people from waiting and seeing, the tax rates will be adjusted according to the fertility of the land when verifying the tax categories, increasing the tax rates for adjacent fields. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 25th)

Shang Zhen Telephones the National Economic Council to Request Funds to Repair the Collapsed Dike at Lengzhai

(Tianjin) Shang Zhen telegraphed the National Economic Council, stating that the dike south of Lengzhai, at the junction of sections three and four on the southern bank of the Yellow River, as well as the Erweipu area in section two, has collapsed and is in a critical situation. If the dike relies on the breach, the sand dike will be extremely difficult to defend against the water. The low-lying areas behind the river are at risk of affecting Shandong and Jiangsu provinces if there is any negligence, and there is a danger of the river changing course southward. Although rescue efforts have been made, it is difficult to raise the necessary funds. Please allocate 200,000 yuan quickly for defense. (Special dispatch from the 25th)

Tianjin National Salvation Fund: Establishment Meeting of the Guarantee Committee Held

(Tianjin) The Tianjin National Salvation Fund Guarantee Committee held its establishment meeting on the afternoon of the 25th, passing the organizational charter. It stipulates that there will be ten committee members, including seven executive committee members and three supervisory committee members, all of whom will be appointed by the municipal government. It is reported that the distribution and use of the fund in the future must be proposed by three or more executive and supervisory committee members and approved by a two-thirds majority of the entire committee before it can be withdrawn. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 25th)

Resolution of the Case of U.S. Navy Sailors in Qinhuangdao Beating a Man to Death

(Tianjin) The case of U.S. sailors from the USS Canopus in Qinhuangdao beating two Chinese men to death has been resolved through negotiations. U.S. Consul Huarui from Tianjin went to Yuguan on the 23rd to visit Su Yuqi, the director of the Public Security Bureau, to formally apologize and provide a written reply. The two sailors involved in the incident have been sent to the headquarters of the Far East Fleet and charged with homicide. Regarding compensation and condolences, the U.S. side has agreed to handle it as requested. (Special dispatch from the 25th)

Major Bandit Luo Shan Shot Dead for Resisting Arrest

(Zhengzhou) The major bandit Shang Yingcu, from Luo Shan, was ordered by the Pacification Commissioner's Office to be pacified by the county, but the bandit's nature was difficult to change. The Pacification Commissioner's Office then dispatched troops to encircle and suppress him. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 21st, the bandit leader Shang Yingcu opened fire to resist arrest, resulting in street fighting. The bandit leader Shang Yingcu's grandson, Sun Zikuan, was shot dead on the spot, and more than ten bandits were captured alive. More than a hundred guns were seized. The troops of Tang Junde are dispatching teams to search and suppress the remnants of the bandits in the countryside. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 25th)

(Xi'an) According to a Lanzhou airmail dispatch, at 3:00 PM on the 20th, the gunpowder depot in Xiadongmen exploded, and the fire continued until the 21st. Hundreds of soldiers and civilians were killed or injured, and hundreds of civilian houses throughout the city were reduced to ashes. The authorities have allocated 30,000 yuan for relief. The cause of the accident was careless placement and the effects of the weather. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 24th)

Although the central government has not yet determined the amount, it has promised to allocate a large sum because Wang, Kong, and Xu all know that the disaster in Hubei is extremely severe and cannot be relieved without a large sum of money. (Special dispatch from the 25th)

Case of Tian Lun Crashing into a Sailing Boat: Japanese Consul Agrees to Investigate and Negotiate

Japanese Economic Observation Group Arrives in Hankou from Shanxi for Inspection; Holds Economic Discussion Meeting with Japanese Merchants; States That the Purpose of the Trip Is to Enhance Goodwill

Hankou Correspondence: The Economic Observation Group, organized and initiated by the Japanese Telegraphic Communication Society, arrived in China amidst high-sounding cries of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. They visited Qingdao, Jinan, Tianjin, Beiping, Zhangjiakou, Datong, and then Taiyuan. On the 23rd, they arrived at Shijiazhuang via the Zhengtai Railway from Taiyuan and transferred to the special express train on the Pinghan Railway southward, arriving in Hankou at 8:00 PM on the 24th. The group consists of fourteen members: Mishima Kaiun, Hirota Kaichi, Ueda Ryoichi, Suzui Masamoto, Suzuki Uichi, Ezaki Riichi, Mesaki Kenji, Fukui Tatsuro, Manaka Tsunehiko, Arakawa Chotaro, Kuroda Nakajo, Kamikosima Goro, Okuhira Minoru, and Kuda Tankai. The group stated that their purpose is to observe the actual conditions of Chinese industry and commerce, adjust the economies of China and Japan, and enhance their goodwill. The results of their observations in Shandong, Hebei, Chahar, and Shanxi provinces have been very fruitful. The group is scheduled to visit the consul general and the head of the Japanese Residents Association on the 25th, then cross the river to visit Chairman Zhang of the Provincial Government and attend a banquet hosted by the Provincial Government. In the afternoon, they will visit Mayor Wu of the Hankou Municipal Government. At 4:00 PM, they will hold an economic discussion meeting with all Japanese merchants at the Japanese Chamber of Commerce and Industry. On the 26th, they will visit the market and visit Chinese business leaders. On the evening of the 27th, they will visit Luojia Mountain in Wuchang and take the Xiangyang Wheel to Nanjing and then Shanghai. (24th)

Songjiang: County Government Establishes People's Information Office

The county government recently followed the regulations of the People's Information Office promulgated by the Ministry of Interior. The newly appointed County Magistrate Li Leng immediately promulgated the detailed rules for the People's Information Office after taking office. From 7:30 AM to 5:00 PM daily, people are allowed to inquire about government policies and other issues. The county magistrate and all department heads personally answer questions sincerely. If a case is more complex, a written reply is provided. Since the office opened, it has resolved several minor disputes among the people, and the public feels it is very convenient.

Suzhou: Water Disaster Relief Performance Funds

The Wu County Relief Water Disaster Branch has spared no effort in raising relief funds. It has already remitted 5,000 yuan. County Magistrate Wu invited leaders from the gentry and business communities to a banquet on the 24th, raising more than 3,000 yuan on the spot. At the same time, he entrusted the Great China Theater to schedule Beijing Opera rehearsals for three days starting on the 26th at Xinwuhui outside Changmen, inviting movie star Ms. Yuan Meiyun to perform on stage. Ms. Yuan arrived in Suzhou from Shanghai at 3:00 PM on the 25th. The Public Security Bureau specially sent a military band to welcome her at the station. The Water Disaster Relief Association continued to hold a meeting on the 25th to discuss methods for collecting house donations. It is reported that famous actor Mei Lanfang will come to Suzhou in early November to perform relief plays for three days. Negotiations are currently underway.

Wuxi: Two-Headed Snake Resembles a Loach

Fei Ashan, a resident of Zuoxiang Lane in Huadafang Village in the third district of the county, captured a strange snake in his patio on the 24th. It is about a foot long, and its body shape resembles a loach, but it has two heads and looks very much like a water snake. When it raises its head and walks, it makes a "hoo-hoo" sound in its mouth, and its eyes are bright and golden. Its appearance is terrifying. The strange snake has now been placed in a glass bottle for viewing. Those who see it are amazed.

Changzhou: Thorough Investigation of the Bandit Arrest Incident

The Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department has dispatched investigator Li Yunmo to Changzhou to investigate the case reported by the Wujin County side regarding the dispatch of a detective team to Shizhuang Town at the border of Wujin and Wucheng to arrest Peng Rong. Both sides have presented their own versions of the situation. Li Yunmo arrived in Changzhou on the evening of the 22nd and first visited County Magistrate Hou to inquire about the situation. In the afternoon of the 23rd, he went to the Public Security Bureau to investigate and brought up Zhang Zhen, the guard in charge, for detailed questioning. He has already gained some clues. He stayed at the Dacheng Hotel in the evening, and County Magistrate Hou and Public Security Bureau Chief Xu both visited to discuss the incident in detail. On the 24th, he went to Cheng to investigate in order to report back to the department.

International Commercial Telegram - Special Commercial Telegram from Reuters, October 25th

Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London gold price today is 141 shillings, 6.5 pence, up three pounds.

British Silver: The London silver market is stable today, with no price movement. The spot price is 29.3125 pence, and the futures price is 129.1875 pence. The United States and India purchased. China is engaged in both buying and selling.

Exchange Rates

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market, someone slightly purchased US dollars this morning. The opening exchange rate between British and American currencies was 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 1 fen, 625 li, which is 125 li lower than the closing rate between the US and Britain yesterday. At noon, it continued to fall by 4375 li, reaching 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 1 fen, 1875 li. An hour later, the price returned to Ah 125 li. There was no change at 2:00 PM.

British-French: The opening price fell by three pounds to 74 francs, 56 centimes. At 1:00 PM, it fell another five pounds. At 2:00 PM, it rose by three pounds to 74 francs, 54 centimes.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The opening price of the New York cotton market was slightly lower. Short selling rose, causing the market price to continue to fall. However, the number of sales was absorbed, and the price returned to the same level as the opening price. The mood turned stable. The Supreme Court's ruling on the regulations of the Agricultural Adjustment Administration is unlikely to be announced before the end of November.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was also quiet. At 1:00 PM, the January futures price rose by one pound to 6.10.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market was quiet this morning. At 1:00 PM, the December futures price rose by 375 li to 6 shillings, 4.875 pence.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened with a better mood due to good overseas telegrams. The price rose by 375 li, but there was some short selling later, and the price fell by 125 li at the time of the telegram. The opening price of coarse grains rose by 125 li, then fell with the wheat market.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market opened stably. The price for January-March futures was 6.5 pence, the same as yesterday's closing price. It rose by 0625 in the afternoon.

New York: New York rubber was firmer this morning. The buying mood was quite common at the opening, and the price rose by nine pounds. Demand was good, and the price continued to rise, but the market turned quiet later.

Securities

New York: The New York stock market opened strong this morning. Road stocks and steel stocks rose especially. Later, the mood was pleasant, and the rising trend continued. Mining stocks were even more so. Although there was profit-taking after the high price, the upward trend was not affected by it. The average price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks opened at 139.64, rising by 22 pounds. The prices are as follows:

Local News

Eurasia Aviation Corporation's Junkers Aircraft: Second Plane Arrived in Shanghai Last Night, Took Off from Berlin on the 31st of Last Month, Longhua Airport Made Initial Trial of Night Flight Equipment, the Aircraft Decided to Join the Shanghai-Chengdu Air Route

The second JU52 Junkers aircraft ordered by Eurasia Aviation Corporation from the German Lufthansa took off from Berlin on the 31st of last month. On the 6th, when landing in Rangoon, the landing gear was damaged. After repairs were completed, it continued its flight from Rangoon the day before yesterday and landed in Hanoi that night. It continued its flight from Hanoi yesterday morning and arrived at Shanghai's Longhua Airport at 6:45 PM. Ms. Zhu Qingmu presented flowers, and General Manager Li Jingcong delivered a welcome speech. A grand banquet is scheduled for tonight. The aircraft will fly on the Shanghai-Chengdu route. Details are as follows:

From Germany to Shanghai

The second Junkers aircraft was piloted by five people: Kaspap, the renowned German pilot and captain, Mayer, the co-pilot, Schnlidr, the mechanic, Falipebarucb, the radio operator, and Schiller, the radio engineer. It took off from Berlin, Germany, on the 31st of last month. When landing in Rangoon on the 6th, the aircraft's landing gear sank into the soft mud of the airport and was damaged. After repairs, it finally completed the work the day before yesterday and continued flying, landing in Hanoi that night. Because the airport there was small, the landing gear sank into the mud again. After finding a way to get it out, fortunately the landing gear was not damaged. It left Hanoi yesterday morning and landed in Hong Kong at 12:00 noon. It left Hong Kong for Shanghai at 2:30 PM.

Airport Equipment

After Eurasia Aviation Corporation received a telegram from Hong Kong reporting the aircraft's status, knowing that the plane would not arrive in Shanghai until 7:00 PM, they specifically opened the searchlights and all night flight equipment previously installed at Longhua Airport for the Nanjing-Shanghai night route. More than a dozen gasoline lamps and reflectors were temporarily installed. The German flag and party flag were hung inside the northeast corner of the civilian houses at the field, and the Republic of China flag and party flag were hung at the entrance. Champagne was placed in the middle. The Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched more than a dozen armed police officers to maintain strict security at the airport.

Welcoming Personnel

Those who went to Longhua Airport last night to welcome the aircraft included: Mr. Fu Kai'er, President of the German Chamber of Commerce, Mr. Si De Ci, representative of the Junkers factory stationed in Shanghai, Mr. Shi Tuo Ke, representative of Lufthansa stationed in Shanghai, Mr. Bo Lu Xun, General Manager of Xiangbao Postal Ship Company, Li Jingcong, Manager of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, Liao Guanxuan, German Secretary, He En, Acting Head of the Aircraft Navigation Group, and more than fifty reporters from Chinese and foreign newspapers. Senior company staff were responsible for hospitality. All welcoming personnel arrived at Longhua Airport before 5:30 PM. When the initial telegram was received from Hong Kong, it was reported that the plane would take off at 12:00 noon and was expected to arrive in Shanghai at 5:30 PM. A later telegram indicated that the departure was changed to 2:30 PM, but there was not enough time to notify the welcoming personnel.

Lights Shining

At 6:15 PM yesterday afternoon, Longhua Airport continuously launched rockets (i.e., signals) inside the field. At the same time, the searchlights were turned on to allow the aircraft to see them from afar, indicating that it was an airport. At 6:45 PM, the sound of an aircraft was suddenly heard at the field. All welcomers looked up and saw that the aircraft was in the air above the airport. Only a large green light could be seen on the right wing. After circling the field once, the aircraft descended. A car dispatched by Eurasia Corporation led the way to the front of the field before stopping. The aircraft was silver-gray, with the large characters (DAges) painted on the fuselage, exactly the same as the first aircraft.

Group Presented Flowers

All welcoming personnel went to the front of the plane. Kaspap, the captain, and Mayer, the co-pilot, and the other five people disembarked one after another. Miss Zhu Qingmu presented flowers and shook hands with the welcoming personnel one by one. General Manager Li Jingquan stepped forward to welcome the pilots and accompanied them to the inside of the reception area, where champagne was served, and a welcome speech was given. At the same time, the welcomers applauded. It ended at 7:20 PM.

Li's Speech

Li Jingcong, General Manager of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, delivered a welcome speech, saying, "Ladies and gentlemen, please allow me to take this opportunity, in the name of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, to express my most sincere welcome to the flight crew of the JU52 aircraft that has just flown to Shanghai. As you all know, we want to conquer the skies between Europe and Asia. Based on the fact that silver aircraft have repeatedly flown directly from Berlin to Shanghai in the past year, we sincerely hope that air transportation between Europe and Asia can be realized in the near future. This is the task we are responsible for, and it is the goal we are striving for. Your arrival has reopened the road of air transportation between Europe and Asia. I can very well use the words of the old Roman general and loudly proclaim, 'You came, you saw, you helped us break through all the obstacles to air transportation between Europe and Asia.' Now, I request everyone to join me in congratulating the flight crew of the Dages aircraft and to wish them good health." The speech was then translated by the German secretary, Liao Huanxuan.

Banquet Tonight

Captain Kaspap and the other five people stayed at the International Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road last night. Eurasia Aviation Corporation is scheduled to hold a grand banquet at 7:00 PM today, probably at the Xinghua Restaurant on Fuzhou Road. Chinese and Western directors of the company, personnel from the German embassy and chamber of commerce, and representatives of Lufthansa Junkers stationed in Shanghai will be invited to attend. It is heard that after the pilots send the aircraft to Eurasia Corporation, they will return to Germany by boat. When they arrived in Shanghai last night, they also brought a personal letter from Lufthansa to Li Jingcong, General Manager of Eurasia Aviation Corporation.

Joining the Air Route

The aircraft is equipped with three engines and is fully equipped. In the future, it will join the Shanghai-Xinjiang and Shaanxi-Chengdu routes, passing through Shanghai, Nanjing, Zhengzhou, Xi'an, Hanzhong, Chengdu, and other places. Flights will depart from Shanghai every Tuesday and Friday and from Chengdu every Wednesday and Saturday.

National Labor Representative Secretary Zhang Daomin Returned to China Yesterday, Examined the Current State of Labor and Rural Economy in Various Countries, Also Expressed Opinions on China's Labor Organization

Shanghai News Agency reports that Wang Jinxia, the labor representative attending the International Labor Conference on behalf of China, has already returned to the country. Secretary Zhang Daomin, after visiting various countries to investigate the state of labor and rural economy, returned to China yesterday aboard the Nagasaki Maru. A reporter from the Shanghai News Agency paid a special visit to Mr. Zhang at the New Asia Hotel. According to the interview, the details are as follows:

Investigation Process

Mr. Zhang went abroad with the National Labor Representative on May 10. On June 4, he attended the International Labor Conference. After the closing on the 26th, he went to Italy, Austria, Czechoslovakia, Germany, Denmark, Belgium, the Netherlands, the United Kingdom, France, Poland, Russia, Japan, and other countries to investigate the current state of labor and rural economy. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday from Japan aboard the Nagasaki Maru. The details of the International Labor Conference have already been reported and published, so they were not discussed.

Conditions in Various Countries

Mr. Zhang first stated that the labor conditions in European countries have already been put on track, especially in the United Kingdom and France. British industry is developed, with a history of more than 80 years. In Germany, all workers, from young to old, if they can work, do not have to worry about not having food to eat. Their labor insurance system is handled very well. The German labor policy is based on the labor front, where labor and capital are integrated. Even under economic panic, there are very few unemployed people, and those who are unemployed can still live, so they can restore economic prosperity. Italy is on the road to labor freedom and labor welfare. Their organization has professional associations, but the welfare of workers is obtained under the interests of the country. Without the interests of the country, the welfare of workers cannot be discussed. The labor situation in Russia is similar to that in Germany, but the system is different. In terms of agriculture, the agricultural cooperation in the Netherlands and the collective farms in Russia have achieved considerable success.

Zhang's Opinion

Compared with Western Europe, China is of course very far behind. However, to seek economic prosperity and industrial development, it is necessary to start from the labor aspect, and China's mechanical workers and agricultural workers cannot be separated. China's economic foundation should be based on agricultural labor, and to obtain the effect of agricultural labor, it is necessary to use agricultural cooperation methods and have a whole plan to organize it. Therefore, China's labor movement must have a new organization in the future, under the overall interests of the country, so that labor and capital can be integrated to obtain true labor interests, he said.

Ministry of Communications Pays Attention to Aviation Equipment

In order to facilitate air transportation, the Ministry of Communications is paying close attention to aviation equipment. It recently issued the following instructions to China National Aviation Corporation: (1) Wireless radio direction finders are necessary for blind flying. The company has not yet universally installed this equipment at important stations, which is not sufficient to ensure flight safety. The company is hereby ordered to promptly install the above-mentioned instruments extensively to facilitate air transportation. This is of utmost importance. (2) Meteorological equipment is extremely important for aviation safety. The company's meteorological observation equipment is only simple equipment, which is not sufficient to meet the needs. How to control the national meteorological agencies so that they can all make aviation meteorological reports to facilitate navigation is currently being handled by the Ministry in consultation with the Aviation Committee. Before the unified method is determined, the company should select important locations on all routes passing through heavy mountains and sea areas with unstable climates and quickly add radio stations and meteorological equipment to facilitate communication and ensure safety. In addition to separate orders, the company is hereby ordered to comply and report accordingly.

Xin Feng Ship Encountered Hurricane on the Way Back to Shanghai, Shaft Broken, Bureau Dispatched Hai Rui to Rescue, Expected to Be Towed Back Safely

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xin Feng ship, a formal North Sea liner, departed from Shanghai for Tianjin at 2:00 PM on the 17th of this month. On the 22nd, it loaded cargo and passengers in Tianjin and departed south for Shanghai, first going to Yantai to load more passengers and cargo. At approximately 7:00 AM yesterday morning, when traveling to 34 degrees 50 minutes North latitude and 122 degrees 17 minutes East longitude, it encountered a hurricane. The captain initially ordered all crew members to fight together. After three hours, at 10:30 AM, the ship's shaft, unable to withstand the impact of the wind and waves, suddenly broke, losing the ability to navigate. The situation was extremely dangerous.

Flying Telegram for Help

The ship was drifting northwest. All the passengers and crew on board were in a state of extreme emergency and panic. The captain sent a most urgent radio telegram for help to Shanghai, requesting the head office to quickly find a way to rescue the ship to protect the lives and property of all on board. The bureau received the alarm telegram in the afternoon, and the chief captain of the shipping department gathered to discuss rescue measures. It was not determined until 5:00 PM.

Dispatch Ship to Tow

The China Merchants Bureau notified the insurance company of the original telegram and gathered the heads of various departments and the chief captain to discuss rescue methods. It was decided that the bureau's Hai Rui ship, which is currently transporting goods in Haizhou Lianyungang, is the closest to the sea area where Xin Feng encountered the accident. It was decided to dispatch the ship from Lao Yao quickly to tow the distressed vessel. After the agreement, a telegram was immediately sent to the captain of the Hai Rui to speed up the voyage. A reply telegram was also sent to the captain of the Xin Feng, awaiting the Hai Rui's rescue. According to Zhao Yuntai, chief of the shipping department, the Xin Feng is expected to be safely towed back to Shanghai by the Hai Rui and there should be no unexpected major risks.

It is heard that the negotiations are very close and there is hope for a resolution. Director Tang will come to Shanghai again in the coming days to discuss everything.
