Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

"Extremely Civilized" Weapons and "Novelties"

— Meng Ruo

It is said that Italy is a civilized country and Abyssinia is a barbaric country, and that is probably correct. We don't need to cite many things as proof; just look at their fight this time, and the weapons used by the two armies, and you can see the difference between civilization and barbarism. The Italian army used poison gas and dumdum bullets to attack the Abyssinian army, while the Abyssinian army used spears and shields to resist the Italian army. The former is a modern new weapon, and the latter is an ancient old weapon. The barbaric country of Abyssinia wants to use the old weapons of ancient times to deal with the modern new weapons of the civilized country of Italy, and the result of being massacred must be inevitable. Who would listen to your barbarism, Abyssinia, that in today's advanced tactics and developed weapons, you still take out spears and try to fight the enemy? You really deserve it!

However, we must say that it is also unfair to say that Italy is a civilized country and Abyssinia is a barbaric country. Take the use of poison gas and dumdum bullets, for example, weren't these two kinds of military supplies banned internationally long ago? But Italy, which is called a civilized country, this time violated the convention and used these two kinds of poisons to harm the Abyssinians. On the other hand, Abyssinia, which is regarded as a barbaric country, did not dare to use them. Here, the true face of the so-called civilized people is fully exposed—

However, although Abyssinia announced to the world the use of poison gas and dumdum bullets, Italy did not admit it. The Abyssinian embassy in England recently issued a statement to refute this, saying that the Italian army's use of this "extremely civilized" weapon has been proven by a member of the Abyssinian foreign medical team, and if the Italian army continues to use this weapon, Abyssinia can no longer prohibit soldiers from using the same weapon. In this way, if the Italian army uses this "extremely civilized" weapon to attack the Abyssinians in the future, Abyssinia will undoubtedly use the same weapon to resist the Italians. By then, the Italian army may also have to taste the taste of the "extremely civilized" weapon.

However, although Abyssinia can also use "extremely civilized" weapons, this is not enough to improve its degree of civilization. How do you say that? It is because the Abyssinians have never seen a movie since they were born. According to news from Tigre yesterday, the Italian army is now enriching its propaganda power with films, and will open a screening in Aduwa city today. This is the first time that the residents of the city have ever seen it since they were born. The content of the film is patriotic demonstrations in Italy and the land and air military exercises held in Bolzano city in nine days, in order to show the strength of Italy. At that time, all Italian generals and soldiers will visit the venue. During the screening, it will also be explained in Amharic. A large number of local natives will visit this "novelty."

It can be seen that Italy not only has "extremely civilized" weapons, but also has "novelties." Can you say that it is not more civilized than Abyssinia?

Illness

— Meng Hua

My younger brother was fired by the manager of his shop because the manager saw blood in his spit.

Naturally, this was a big blow to us. This fixed income of eighteen yuan per month was lost along with the manager's announcement. Originally, I relied mostly on my younger brother, but now I have to take on this burden of life, because I am older than him and my illness is lighter. Needless to say, there is no room for discussion, I have to quietly and reluctantly take over this burden.

Unfortunately, due to the stimulation of unemployment and the lack of security in life, my younger brother's insomnia, which had been cured, attacked him again. At night, when I heard him tossing and turning, and his low cough, I also opened my eyes and looked at the mosquito net, looking at everything in the room, until dawn. But my younger brother's cheeks were even redder and scarier, and his lips were dry and scorched.

So, we had to come to the countryside, and this refreshing and fresh air was a bit beneficial to us. The countryside is quiet, and our house is bathed in the middle of the fields. Every day, my younger brother's coughing sound, following the rhythmic ticking of the clock on the table, played a poignant and melancholy tune. At night, the autumn insects along the wall also flapped their wings and sang their elegy. This dying scream accompanied the low cough, relentlessly piercing my heart.

The house is close to the railroad, and dozens of trains pass by here every day. At first, it is faint, and then it comes with a ground-shaking force, and the walls shake as well. The sharp whistle and the roaring sound of the train make me roll or put down my pen every time, and listen quietly, inexplicably, and fascinatedly.

"Fourth brother, when I hear the train, I think of..." my younger brother said. I understand what he means. Although my younger brother is sick, his thoughts and desires are as usual, and even stronger. He is exactly the same as me. Listening to this earth-shattering sound, his heart has already flown far away.

In this situation, my mood is depressed and indignant. What is forcing us to do this? The burden of life, excessive labor, everything has eroded my younger brother's life, making some of his organs gradually rot and gradually destroy. It is going to take away his life, his happiness, and even his hope.

Tonight, under the dim light, I bravely picked up my pen and decided to write something. I thought that if I didn't have money to send him to the hospital for treatment, I should at least buy him a bottle of cod liver oil, because it is not okay for him to continue like this. But what can I write? His coughing sounds like a sharp knife, ruthlessly dragging my heart. I looked at the light sadly and indignantly, lost in thought.

"Fourth brother, take a break. Don't ruin your health either," my younger brother said suddenly.

I turned my head. The mosquito net on the bed was hanging up and down, sadly. I saw my younger brother looking at me very excitedly, his eyes like a torch, burning my heart. He put one hand on his chest and gasped. I hurriedly got up and poured him a glass of water. He sat up and said in a low voice, "I'm already sick. If you get sick too, we two won't be able to survive!"

"Don't worry, just take care of yourself. Don't think about anything that's not good. Your body doesn't allow you to think wildly. Look at how much worse your insomnia has become. Just think about their future, and you'll be happy. Don't think wildly!" I comforted him. I saw strings of clear tears dripping from the corners of his eyes. The autumn insects were calling sadly, and the wind in the field was playing a tragic tune, along with my younger brother's coughing sound.

I went back to my seat, opened the paper, and bravely picked up my pen again. "Life is forcing you to write. You have to think about the doctor and the cod liver oil!" I encouraged myself. So I tried my best to write.

I woke up in the middle of the night, and my younger brother was still not asleep. "Younger brother, are you still not asleep?" I asked him in surprise.

"No, I just woke up," he said. Obviously, this was a cover-up. He immediately turned over and pretended to snore.

"This can't go on," I thought. "Poverty is our shadow. It is something that follows us every step of the way. But we are not afraid of him at all, just like the many people in the world who have hope and will. But such a body, this fatal disease, has deprived us of everything. Even if winter passes, it will be spring, but can my younger brother's body survive this cruel winter? A nineteen-year-old youth

Page 21

, he has such a great future, but the demons are forcing him, watching him about to die. How cruel this is!" So my eyes became a little moist again.

Gloomy Days

— Ji Xuan

"Plants born in the shade, if not transplanted by human hands, must spend their entire lives in that shade, those gloomy days; but fortunately, humans can seize the endlessly endowed natural tonic. Sunlight not only gives good results to the body, but also has a great impact on the spirit. Just looking up at the azure sky from a sickbed will make you feel very happy, so being in the entire sunlight is bound to get the supreme pleasure." — (Kojima Fujiki)

In days when life has lost its center, in endless sorrow and decadence, one's own fragile soul is almost being stirred by the destroying black hand, planning to follow it and hide in an unknown world, I saw those few words in a small booklet.

As if a high-voltage current passed through, the nerves were hit hard, and in a kind of unprepared fluster, I froze; I pondered these strange sentences.

Simple, plain, real and unadorned words, what a wonderful and incomprehensible revelation it gives to a soul living in gloomy days?

As if gaining some valuable emotions from here, a kind of gratitude gushed up like an ancient hot spring, and a kind of innate stubbornness lurking deep in the soul erupted like a volcano. At this time, I began to feel angry, and also felt ashamed.

"When a plant is transplanted in the shade, it can only spend its life of gloomy days there." In this era, perhaps countless souls, like myself, have been transplanted to the shade, and are living endless "gloomy days"? However, what is transplanted in the end is the "soul", a part of humanity, not a plant without mouth, eyes, hands and feet. Life is fierce, and that series of "gloomy days" is also terrible; however, think about it: it is a person, not a "plant" that can be transplanted at will; dominating life is human beings themselves, and it is not said that what dominates human beings is terrible life!

A kind of shame, a kind of anger, a kind of self-confidence and pride (it is "human pride"), rose vaguely like the warm moisture on the muddy ground in March. One's own family has been transplanted to a shady place where sunlight cannot be seen, and is living in "gloomy days": but, picking up a mirror to look at, youthful stubbornness is still indelibly engraved on the thin face. "Not a tender and ignorant plant, it should not be transplanted at will," that thought.

So, looking out of the dark and narrow room again: the sky is blue, the sea is vast, and the sun is still shining there on the other side of the mountain: isn't there still a place in the outside world that is bright and warm with sunlight? Isn't that...?

Thinking, the pressure given to me by the gloomy days in front of me seems to be much lighter. It no longer seems so heavy, firm, dark and suffocating to me: it no longer has the face of a dominating master and a demon king to me; I learned the trick of taking it lightly, I learned to use "anger and stubbornness with sparks cracking"!

Yes, not a small plant, but human beings! Isn't it said? "What humans are fortunate about is that they can use their own will to seize this natural health tonic—sunlight." Yes, that is human pride! Looking out at the blue sky from an unhealthy sickbed can already make people feel happy, and what if they can be in the boundless light seized by their own strength...?

Life, use your last bit of strength to transplant people into the shade! Gloomy days, you also use all your baseness!

People are not plants—people have their own happiness and endowment.

Loneliness

— Er He

Because it was Sunday, I woke up a little late in the morning. The tea house brought the soybean milk and said it was about to get cold, so I rubbed my sleepy eyes and got up quickly. I didn't have time to wash my face or brush my teeth, so I finished the soybean milk and soybean curd. I thought, you are the best tonic, much more effective than cod liver oil, etc. So I licked my lips with the tip of my tongue for a while, and felt that the taste was indeed strong.

When I came back from a walk, I saw that the sun had already shone through the top of the cypress tree in front of the door. I glanced at the desk and saw a pile of homework like a small mountain. I thought, I don't care about it. So I lay down in the reclining chair and didn't want to smoke, but felt silent and empty in my heart. I fantasized for a while, and my about-to-be-destroyed soul was stirring again. Ah, I feel lonely. This loneliness is even impossible to dispel. I know very well that I have a lot of work to do on the desk, and it is beneficial to people and myself to clean up these odds and ends on Sunday. Is the whip of Monday about to lash out? But I just lay silently in the reclining chair, not wanting to do anything. I just endured the unbearable loneliness, and my heart was bottomless empty.

I was too lazy to go to the office for the prescribed two hours of office work, and preferred to be in the lonely house,

Page 22

Enduring the unbearable loneliness. Looking out from the front window, the lawn, although dyed by autumn, was still green, which made me feel more sorrowful about my old age. Sparrows often chirped on the ancient rafters of the Confucius Temple, but this not only failed to break the loneliness, but also increased the heaviness of loneliness. Sometimes, they jumped down on the grass as if they had fallen abstractly, and the sound of "ga" made me wake up and look over, thinking it was the sound of uninvited guests. Yes, at this time, I desperately hope that someone will come to talk, and I will treat him with a cigarette and a glass of plain water. I will tell him how lonely I feel, but just talking about loneliness, in loneliness, I can get rid of loneliness. But where are my friends? So I raised my head and looked at the white clouds in the sky. The white clouds must be floating over the Yangtze River, and the white clouds must be floating over the top of the big city? Then, it should have seen my friends. What are my friends doing in the pigeon-like houses? Maybe they are also looking at the white clouds in the sky? Thinking, the feeling of loneliness became stronger and stronger. So I couldn't help but smoke. In the curling smoke, I saw many ethereal dreams.... So I don't know where the chattering sparrows flew to, but the loneliness became heavier. So I thought of a foreign writer's "Affair in the Desert." A French sailor was captured by the Arabs, and fled at night, but lost his way and walked into a desert. Then he met a female leopard. In loneliness, he and the female leopard were like a pair of lovers. I do need any kind of creature, cat, leopard..., but even the chattering sparrows that just came don't know where they flew to. So I spit out smoke, let the thick, lingering smoke occupy this lonely room.

After lunch, I fell on the bed like a dying cold butterfly. When I woke up, I felt that the afternoon dream was also lonely. I saw that the sun had shone through the back window a lot. I was lying in the reclining chair, looking at the pile of homework on the table like a small mountain, but just silently. When it comes to the most lonely time, what can I do to get rid of it? I can't do any work. How can I get through the late and lonely time by sitting? Looking at the sunlight on the white wall in the house gradually lengthening, but how old that is, is the late autumn sun already old?

Outside the window, a gentle gust of wind occasionally blew and turned a few pages of the books on the table, but then closed by itself again. The sunlight on the wall always moves slowly. Looking, looking, I just think someone will knock on my door. Other than that, I just think that dusk will come a little faster, but what follows dusk is a long night...

Sending Xinglong

Huiling (1380) 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening the Curtain "Spring Outing" (Each sentence embeds names of characters from Dream of the Red Chamber)

"Daiyu girl is the most affectionate. Today's attire is for 'Visiting Spring.' She wears a 'Zijuan' shirt, and a 'Cuilu' skirt, adorned with a phoenix to resemble 'Keqing.' Leading the 'Li Wen' and 'Li Qi' maids, she moves gracefully onto the boat like 'Xiangling.' 'Untying the rope,' she drifts on the lake, with 'Yuanyang' playing in the green waves. Recalling last year when 'Xueyan' flew into the reeds. Before long, willows 'Connect' and 'Welcome Spring' again. Sadly, the peaches on 'Little Paper' are not yet ripe, but one hears 'Ying'er's' cry from the treetops. The setting sun resembles 'Amber.' A gentle breeze 'Assaults People with Flowers.' The boat docks at 'Embroidery Orange' Temple to visit the 'Miaoyu' nun and discuss the past and present. Crossing the 'A Little Board' bridge and 'Rainbow Cloud' path, one hears a 'Quiet Bell' cleanse the heart. She knits and strikes the 'Precept Ring,' and 'Granny Liu' responds by opening the fight. Inviting her to sit in the 'Baoyu' Pavilion, she is presented with a cup of tea, 'Pine Branch' and 'Baking Tea.' Incense from the furnace 'Xiu Yan' and 'Hui Xiang.' The 'Dou Qin' zither on the table is silent. The distant landscape is like being 'In the Book,' and the little magpies return to their nests like 'Gathering Clouds.' After a brief chat, she returns home, and one sees the 'Musk Moon' shining upwards. With a 'Hulala' sound, the water 'Xiang Yun's'."

Leftovers

"In the current decline of the singing world, only Metropolis Society can maintain its purity." What Nelson calls purity, I don't know how to interpret it?

And saying that a singer who sings well and is not arrogant, then "only" Miss Jingyun, is a bit too much and has the flavor of yelling and cheering.

Praising also has to be done properly, otherwise, if you praise to the high heavens, the one being praised will also have a headache and goosebumps!

The broadcaster, Xu XX, published an article in the broadcasting magazine a month ago, saying that "Lingjin Society owes electricity bills," etc., but afterward, the president of the society indiscriminately said he wanted to "find me" to talk, and God knows what that means!

Bai Xue: Willing to cooperate with you, but I have to declare that I have a strange habit of internal strife. If Bai Xue is a strange thing like Cao Cao, then I will go to war with He!

Page 23

Zeng Ren, who is usually most afraid of dancing, has also been seen frequently in dance halls recently, accompanied by Yuan Fengju from China Radio. This is also a strange thing! (Above miscellaneous)

The private broadcasting charity performance has been over for many days, and the accounts have not yet been made public, which is very worrying.

It is said that Mr. Yuan Fengju, the host of this Chinese event, spent a huge sum of 1,400 yuan on ticket sales, and even rushed to put on the play "Xiao He Chasing Han Xin" within a month. This gentleman has always been thorough in his work. When he took over Huaxing Radio, the three-day special program made him famous at sea, and when he took over China Radio, he also excelled with special programs. Therefore, the result of this charity event should be more colorful than the film industry's disaster relief! (Above Jin Lang)

Yesterday, I hired a car to Foyin Radio and played there for more than an hour. It happened to be the broadcasting program of the Era Opera Company. I met all of their members and got many pleasant conversations, for example: Miss Wang Qi: Can be purely said to be a girl who understands the fun of singing. She has a healthy physique and is indeed not comparable to those who rely on the power of cosmetics to seduce young masters. I asked her why she was broadcasting? She replied with a smile: Happy!

Lin Ying: If you see her occasionally, you will definitely think she is an adult, but in fact, she is still a very lively child! She told me that she was only replacing Ye Ying and Ye Hong, who had gone to Siam.

Zhu Shuya is their president. The look on his face when sorting out the music was really like he couldn't find the lottery ticket. But in the end, he was still urged by the friends in the band. Alas! He's already considered enthusiastic.

Ji Jianhun: Enthusiastically jumping like a little monkey. Thanks to his thorough arrangements, otherwise, the lady's temper would be really terrible. This is because he is the leader of the singing group.

Fang Lan: Only sixteen years old, her methods are as sophisticated as the songs she sings. She is a top student at an obstetrics school. The drama group is led by Liu Yawei, and the members include Yan Qun, Xu Jingya and her brother Jingsheng, Jin Jin, and Liang Dusheng.

Mr. Liu told me that the members also include Liu Liying, Cang Yinqiu, Wei Heling, and Gao Mangsheng. The people who perform the broadcast are often changed, with the purpose of gathering interest. Business is secondary. After broadcasting "Yang Guifei," they plan to adapt the film script "The Peach Blossom Fan," which will probably be realized before the end of the month.

This group, in addition to the veterans who have always had broadcasting experience, are friends who are very accomplished on the stage or in the movies. I hope that they will not only take the interest of gathering as a premise, but also take on the educational spirit under possible circumstances to increase the strength of social education. (A Li)

Mr. Xu Jingsheng, the former chief playwright of the Guanyin Drama Company, has now officially joined the Era Broadcasting Opera Company as a playwright. However, Mr. Xu's entry and exit from the radio station are closely monitored by his fiancée, Miss Fang Yun. (Secret Agent)

Mr. Wu Zhanda sent a letter to Qian Yujun, saying: "... But it is true that the wedding invitations of the Zhu family were sent on behalf of the Zhu family, and it was not a whim. It was Mr. Zhou Gongjun, the former leader of a certain troupe in our society, who discussed with the troupe to perform as guest performers, and it was true that the ladies of the troupe allowed it..." (Original letter), etc., is specially reprinted here, just to clarify.

Movie News

Silver Jottings

— Zhi Er

Zhang Xinzhu, the new talent of Diantong introduced by Yuan Muzhi, the "old customer," originally had a one-year contract with Diantong. Now it is said that the contract will be torn up halfway through because Diantong believes that Zhang Xinzhu's performance in "City Scenery" is not good, and Zhang Xinzhu's appearance on the screen was originally for "self-promotion," so after one movie was filmed, she was already satisfied and didn't want to continue.

Diantong will stage a play "Resurrection" once, which is now in full swing. It is said that the script is being adapted by Tang Na based on the original.

After the drama movement, it seems to have become a sideline trend for various film companies. The "Crescent Moon" of the stars has already been staged. The Yueming Company has the Oriental Theatre Company led by Wan Laitian and Jinshan, and Tianyi and Yihua have recently been rumored to have theatre company organizations as well. The only one missing is the Lianhua Company.

It is said that Ouyang Yuqian, one of the three playwrights for the stars, has written a story and will send it to Beijing for preliminary review in the near future. As for the other two, Liu Na and others, there is still no news.

About The Inspector General

"The Inspector General" (i.e., the Imperial Envoy), directed by Sun Shiyi, Shen Xicen, Gao Laitian, Zhang Min, and Shi Dongshan, has been scheduled to be staged at the Jincheng Grand Theatre starting on the first of next month. With only one week left, the directing team yesterday issued an urgent notice, stipulating that rehearsals will be held every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday until the end of the show. The actors have no difficulty and are in good spirits.

Shi Chao, the protagonist of Liberty God, plays a principal in "The Inspector General," who is timid as a mouse.

Gu Menghu knowingly breaks the law. In "The Inspector General," as the director of the post office, he secretly opens the letters of the Imperial Envoy and exposes the secrets of the Imperial Envoy.

"The Inspector General" is dubbed by Lü Ji and lit by Yang Qiming. It is currently being studied in the hope that this performance will make a new contribution.

Miss Wang Ying and Miss Ye Luqian have recently been making a fuss out of jealousy. It is because the mother and daughter in "The Inspector General" are both in love with the "Imperial Envoy," which is not true. Zhao Dan can rest assured.

Jinshan has read the script of "The Inspector General" thoroughly.

Zheng Junli and Zuo Mingjin are suffering unspeakably, having to film and rush to rehearse "The Inspector General."

Lan Ping, who was the wealthy and noble Mrs. Helmer in "A Doll's House," is a carpenter's wife in "The Inspector General," who is destitute.

Gu Er and Wang Ying have been very close recently. It is because in "The Inspector General," one plays the county magistrate and the other plays the county magistrate's wife. Little Lulu sees it, I don't know what to think.

Bu Wancang has full confidence in "Triumphant Song."
